<h2 id="setup" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#setup"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Setup</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To use the Toast component, create the toast engine using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">createToaster</code> function.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">This function manages the placement and grouping of toasts, and provides a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">toast</code> object needed to create toast
notification.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> toaster</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> createToaster</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  placement: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;bottom-end&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  overlap: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">true</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  gap: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">24</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">})</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Here&#x27;s an example of creating a toast using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">toast.create</code> method.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8lhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8lhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8lhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="types" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#types"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Types</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can create different types of toasts (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">success</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">error</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">warning</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">info</code>) with appropriate styling. For example,
to create a success toast, you can do:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">toaster.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">success</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  title: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Success!&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  description: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Your changes have been saved.&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">})</span></span></code></pre>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="promise" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#promise"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Promise</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">toaster.promise()</code> to automatically handle the different states of an asynchronous operation. It provides
options for the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">success</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">error</code>, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">loading</code> states of the promise and will automatically update the toast when the
promise resolves or rejects.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="update" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#update"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Update</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To update a toast, use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">toast.update</code> method.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="action" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#action"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Action</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To add an action to a toast, use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">toast.action</code> property.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="duration" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#duration"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Duration</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can control how long a toast stays visible by setting a custom <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">duration</code> in milliseconds, or use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Infinity</code> to keep
it visible until manually dismissed.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="max-visible" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#max-visible"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Max Visible</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">max</code> prop on the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">createToaster</code> function to define the maximum number of toasts that can be rendered at any
one time. Any extra toasts will be queued and rendered when a toast has been dismissed.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="placement" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#placement"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Placement</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Configure where toasts appear on the screen using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">placement</code> option in <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">createToaster</code>. Options include
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">top-start</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">top-end</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">bottom-start</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">bottom-end</code>, and more.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="toast-in-effects" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#toast-in-effects"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Toast in Effects</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When creating a toast inside React effects (like <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useEffect</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useLayoutEffect</code>, or event handlers that trigger during
render), you may encounter a &quot;flushSync&quot; warning. To avoid this, wrap the toast call in <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">queueMicrotask</code>:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">import</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { useEffect } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">from</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;react&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">export</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> const</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> EffectToast</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> () </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">  useEffect</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(() </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">    // ❌ This may cause flushSync warnings</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">    // toaster.create({ title: &#x27;Effect triggered!&#x27; })</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">    // ✅ Wrap in queueMicrotask to avoid warnings</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">    queueMicrotask</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(() </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      toaster.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">create</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        title: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Effect triggered!&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        description: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;This toast was called safely from an effect&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        type: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;success&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }, [])</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  return</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">div</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;Component content&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">div</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">This ensures the toast creation is deferred until after the current execution context, preventing React&#x27;s concurrent
rendering warnings.</p>
<h3 id="styling" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#styling"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Styling</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">There&#x27;s a minimal styling required for the toast to work correctly.</p>
<h4 id="toast-root" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#toast-root"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Toast root</h4>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The toast root will be assigned these css properties at runtime:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--x</code> - The x position</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--y</code> - The y position</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--scale</code> - The scale</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--z-index</code> - The z-index</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--height</code> - The height</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--opacity</code> - The opacity</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--gap</code> - The gap between toasts</li>
</ul>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-scope</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;toast&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;root&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  translate</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--x</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--y</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  scale</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--scale</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  z-index</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--z-index</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  height</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--height</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  opacity</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--opacity</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  will-change</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: translate, opacity, scale;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  transition</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    translate </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">400</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">ms</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    scale </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">400</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">ms</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    opacity </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">400</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">ms</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    height </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">400</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">ms</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    box-shadow </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">200</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">ms</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  transition-timing-function</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">cubic-bezier</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0.21</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">1.02</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0.73</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">1</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &amp;[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-state</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">=&#x27;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">closed</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&#x27;] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    transition</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      translate </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">400</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">ms</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      scale </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">400</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">ms</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      opacity </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">200</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">ms</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    transition-timing-function</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">cubic-bezier</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0.06</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0.71</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0.55</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">1</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="styling-based-on-type" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#styling-based-on-type"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Styling based on type</h4>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can also style based on the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-type</code> attribute.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-scope</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;toast&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;root&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &amp;[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-type</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">=&#x27;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">error</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&#x27;] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    background</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">red</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    color</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">white</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &amp;[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-type</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;info&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    background</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">blue</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    color</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">white</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &amp;[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-type</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;warning&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    background</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">orange</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &amp;[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-type</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;success&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    background</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">green</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    color</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">white</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="mobile-considerations" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#mobile-considerations"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Mobile considerations</h4>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">A very common use case is to adjust the toast width on mobile so it spans the full width of the screen.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">@media</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> (</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">max-width</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">640</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">px</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  [</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-scope</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;toast&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;group&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    width</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">100</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">%</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  [</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-scope</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;toast&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;root&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    inset-inline</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    width</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">calc</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">100</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">%</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> -</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--gap</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">*</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> 2</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><p class="text c_fg.muted">Renders a <code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&lt;div&gt;</code> element.</p><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm overlapping</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">ActionTrigger</h3><p class="text c_fg.muted">Renders a <code class="code code--size_sm Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"toast\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\nconst toaster = createToaster({ placement: 'bottom-end' })\n\n\u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n  {(toast) =\u003e (\n    \u003cToast.Root\u003e\n      \u003cToast.Title /\u003e\n      \u003cToast.Description /\u003e\n      \u003cToast.ActionTrigger /\u003e\n      \u003cToast.CloseTrigger /\u003e\n    \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n  )}\n\u003c/Toaster\u003e\n```\n\n## Setup\n\nTo use the Toast component, create the toast engine using the `createToaster` function.\n\nThis function manages the placement and grouping of toasts, and provides a `toast` object needed to create toast\nnotification.\n\n```ts\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  overlap: true,\n  gap: 24,\n})\n```\n\n## Examples\n\nHere's an example of creating a toast using the `toast.create` method.\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/react/toast'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  overlap: true,\n  gap: 24,\n})\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        className={button.Root}\n        onClick={() =\u003e\n          toaster.create({\n            title: 'Scheduled for tomorrow',\n            description: 'Your meeting has been scheduled for tomorrow at 10am.',\n            type: 'info',\n          })\n        }\n      \u003e\n        Schedule meeting\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root key={toast.id} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e{toast.title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e{toast.description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/solid/toast'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button true,\n    gap: 24,\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        class={button.Root}\n        onClick={() =\u003e\n          toaster.create({\n class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/vue/toast'\nimport { X } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  overlap: true,\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nconst createToast = () =\u003e {\n  toaster.create({\n    title: 'Scheduled for tomorrow',\n    description: 'Your meeting has been scheduled for tomorrow at 10am.',\n    type: 'info',\n  })\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"createToast\"\u003eSchedule meeting\u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cToaster :toaster=\"toaster\" v-slot=\"toast\"\u003e\n        \u003cToast.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003e{{ toast.title }}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e{{ toast.description }}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/svelte/toast'\n  import { X } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    overlap: true,\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  function addToast() {\n    toaster.create({\n      title: 'Scheduled for tomorrow',\n      description: 'Your meeting has been scheduled for tomorrow at 10am.',\n      type: 'info',\n    })\n  }\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv\u003e\n  \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={addToast}\u003eSchedule meeting\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cToaster {toaster}\u003e\n      {#snippet children(toast)}\n        \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Types\n\nYou can create different types of toasts (`success`, `error`, `warning`, `info`) with appropriate styling. For example,\nto create a success toast, you can do:\n\n```ts\ntoaster.success({\n  title: 'Success!',\n  description: 'Your changes have been saved.',\n})\n```\n\n**Example: types**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/react/toast'\nimport { CircleAlertIcon, TriangleAlertIcon, CircleCheckIcon, InfoIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  overlap: true,\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nconst iconMap = {\n  success: CircleCheckIcon,\n  error: CircleAlertIcon,\n  warning: TriangleAlertIcon,\n  info: InfoIcon,\n}\n\nexport const Types = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          className={button.Root}\n          onClick={() =\u003e\n            toaster.success({ title: 'Changes saved', description: 'Your profile has been updated successfully.' })\n          }\n        \u003e\n          Success\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          className={button.Root}\n          onClick={() =\u003e\n            toaster.error({ title: 'Upload failed', description: 'There was an error uploading your file.' })\n          }\n        \u003e\n          Error\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          className={button.Root}\n          onClick={() =\u003e\n            toaster.warning({ title: 'Low storage', description: 'You have less than 10% storage remaining.' })\n          }\n        \u003e\n          Warning\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          className={button.Root}\n          onClick={() =\u003e\n            toaster.info({ title: 'Update available', description: 'A new version of the app is ready to install.' })\n          }\n        \u003e\n          Info\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e {\n            const ToastIcon = toast.type ? iconMap[toast.type as keyof typeof iconMap] : undefined\n            return (\n              \u003cToast.Root key={toast.id} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n                \u003cToast.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e\n                  {ToastIcon \u0026\u0026 \u003cToastIcon className={styles.Indicator} /\u003e}\n                  {toast.title}\n                \u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n                \u003cToast.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e{toast.description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n                \u003cToast.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                  \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n            )\n          }}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/solid/toast'\nimport { CircleAlertIcon, CircleCheckIcon, InfoIcon, TriangleAlertIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Dynamic } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst iconMap = {\n  success: CircleCheckIcon,\n  error: CircleAlertIcon,\n  warning: TriangleAlertIcon,\n  info: InfoIcon,\n}\n\nexport const Types = () =\u003e {\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    overlap: true,\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', 'flex-wrap': 'wrap' }}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          class={button.Root}\n          onClick={() =\u003e\n            toaster.success({ title: 'Changes saved', description: 'Your profile has been updated successfully.' })\n          }\n        \u003e\n          Success\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          class={button.Root}\n          onClick={() =\u003e\n            toaster.error({ title: 'Upload failed', description: 'There was an error uploading your file.' })\n          }\n        \u003e\n          Error\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          class={button.Root}\n          onClick={() =\u003e\n            toaster.warning({ title: 'Low storage', description: 'You have less than 10% storage remaining.' })\n          }\n        \u003e\n          Warning\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          Info\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e {\n            const icon = () =\u003e (toast().type ? iconMap[toast().type as keyof typeof iconMap] : InfoIcon)\n            return (\n              \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n                \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e\n                  \u003cDynamic component={icon()} class={styles.Indicator} /\u003e\n                  {toast().title}\n                \u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n                \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n                \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                  \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n            )\n          }}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/vue/toast'\nimport { InfoIcon,\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; gap: 12px; flex-wrap: wrap\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        :class=\"button.Root\"\n        @click=\"toaster.success({ title: 'Changes saved', description: 'Your profile has been updated successfully.' })\"\n      \u003e\n        Success\n your file.' })\"\n      \u003e\n        Error\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        :class=\"button.Root\"\n        @click=\"toaster.warning({ title: 'Low
