     \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cToaster :toaster=\"toaster\" v-slot=\"toast\"\u003e\n        \u003cToast.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003e\n            \u003ccomponent\n              :is=\"toast.type ? iconMap[toast.type as keyof typeof iconMap] : InfoIcon\"\n              :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\n            /\u003e\n            {{ toast.title }}\n          \u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e{{ toast.description }}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/svelte/toast'\n  import { CircleAlertIcon, TriangleAlertIcon, CircleCheckIcon, InfoIcon, X } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    overlap: true,\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  const iconMap = {\n    success: CircleCheckIcon,\n    error: CircleAlertIcon,\n    warning: TriangleAlertIcon,\n    info: InfoIcon,\n  }\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv\u003e\n  \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; gap: 12px; flex-wrap: wrap;\"\u003e\n    \u003cbutton\n      type=\"button\"\n      class={button.Root}\n      onclick={() =\u003e\n        toaster.success({ title: 'Changes saved', description: 'Your profile has been updated successfully.' })}\n    \u003e\n      Success\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cbutton\n      type=\"button\"\n      class={button.Root}\n      onclick={() =\u003e toaster.error({ title: 'Upload failed', description: 'There was an error uploading your file.' })}\n    \u003e\n      Error\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cbutton\n      type=\"button\"\n      class={button.Root}\n      onclick={() =\u003e\n        toaster.warning({ title: 'Low storage', description: 'You have less than 10% storage remaining.' })}\n    \u003e\n      Warning\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cbutton\n      type=\"button\"\n      class={button.Root}\n      onclick={() =\u003e\n        toaster.info({ title: 'Update available', description: 'A new version of the app is ready to install.' })}\n    \u003e\n      Info\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cToaster {toaster}\u003e\n      {#snippet children(toast)}\n        {@const icon = toast().type ? iconMap[toast().type as keyof typeof iconMap] : InfoIcon}\n        \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e\n            \u003csvelte:component this={icon} class={styles.Indicator} /\u003e\n            {toast().title}\n          \u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Promise\n\nYou can use `toaster.promise()` to automatically handle the different states of an asynchronous operation. It provides\noptions for the `success`, `error`, and `loading` states of the promise and will automatically update the toast when the\npromise resolves or rejects.\n\n**Example: promise-toast**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/react/toast'\nimport { XIcon, LoaderIcon, CircleCheckIcon, CircleAlertIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  overlap: true,\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nconst uploadFile = () =\u003e {\n  return new Promise\u003cvoid\u003e((resolve, reject) =\u003e {\n    setTimeout(() =\u003e {\n      Math.random() \u003e 0.5 ? resolve() : reject(new Error('Upload failed'))\n    }, 2000)\n  })\n}\n\nexport const PromiseToast = () =\u003e {\n  const handleUpload = async () =\u003e {\n    toaster.promise(uploadFile, {\n      loading: {\n        title: 'Uploading file...',\n        description: 'Please wait while we upload your document.',\n      },\n      success: {\n        title: 'Upload complete',\n        description: 'Your file has been uploaded successfully.',\n      },\n      error: {\n        title: 'Upload failed',\n        description: 'Could not upload the file. Please try again.',\n      },\n    })\n  }\n\n  const getIcon = (type: string | undefined) =\u003e {\n    switch (type) {\n      case 'loading':\n        return \u003cLoaderIcon className={styles.Indicator} data-type=\"loading\" /\u003e\n      case 'success':\n        return \u003cCircleCheckIcon className={styles.Indicator} /\u003e\n      case 'error':\n        return \u003cCircleAlertIcon className={styles.Indicator} /\u003e\n      default:\n        return null\n    }\n  }\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cbutton type=\"button\" className={button.Root} onClick={handleUpload}\u003e\n        Upload file\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root key={toast.id} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e\n                {getIcon(toast.type)}\n                {toast.title}\n              \u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e{toast.description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/solid/toast'\nimport { CircleAlertIcon, CircleCheckIcon, InfoIcon, LoaderIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Dynamic } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst uploadFile = () =\u003e {\n  return new Promise\u003cvoid\u003e((resolve, reject) =\u003e {\n    setTimeout(() =\u003e {\n      Math.random() \u003e 0.5 ? resolve() : reject(new Error('Upload failed'))\n    }, 2000)\n  })\n}\n\nconst iconMap = {\n  loading: LoaderIcon,\n  success: CircleCheckIcon,\n  error: CircleAlertIcon,\n  info: InfoIcon,\n}\n\nexport const PromiseToast = () =\u003e {\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    overlap: true,\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  const handleUpload = async () =\u003e {\n    toaster.promise(uploadFile, {\n      loading: {\n        title: 'Uploading file...',\n        description: 'Please wait while we process your file.',\n      },\n      success: {\n        title: 'Upload complete',\n        description: 'Your file has been uploaded successfully.',\n      },\n      error: {\n        title: 'Upload failed',\n        description: 'There was an error uploading your file. Please try again.',\n      },\n    })\n  }\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onClick={handleUpload}\u003e\n        Upload file\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e {\n            const icon = () =\u003e (toast().type ? iconMap[toast().type as keyof typeof iconMap] : InfoIcon)\n            return (\n              \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n                \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e\n                  \u003cDynamic\n                    component={icon()}\n                    class={styles.Indicator}\n                    style={toast().type === 'loading' ? { animation: 'spin 1s linear infinite' } : {}}\n                  /\u003e\n                  {toast().title}\n                \u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n                \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n                \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                  \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n            )\n          }}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/vue/toast'\nimport { X, LoaderIcon, CircleCheckIcon, CircleAlertIcon, InfoIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  overlap: true,\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nconst uploadFile = () =\u003e {\n  return new Promise\u003cvoid\u003e((resolve, reject) =\u003e {\n    setTimeout(() =\u003e {\n      Math.random() \u003e 0.5 ? resolve() : reject(new Error('Upload failed'))\n    }, 2000)\n  })\n}\n\nconst handleUpload = async () =\u003e {\n  toaster.promise(uploadFile, {\n    loading: {\n      title: 'Uploading file...',\n      description: 'Please wait while we process your file.',\n    },\n    success: {\n      title: 'Upload complete',\n      description: 'Your file has been uploaded successfully.',\n    },\n    error: {\n      title: 'Upload failed',\n      description: 'There was an error uploading your file. Please try again.',\n    },\n  })\n}\n\nconst iconMap = {\n  loading: LoaderIcon,\n  success: CircleCheckIcon,\n  error: CircleAlertIcon,\n  info: InfoIcon,\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"handleUpload\"\u003eUpload file\u003c/button\u003e\n\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cToaster :toaster=\"toaster\" v-slot=\"toast\"\u003e\n        \u003cToast.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003e\n            \u003ccomponent\n              :is=\"toast.type ? iconMap[toast.type as keyof typeof iconMap] : InfoIcon\"\n              :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\n              :style=\"toast.type === 'loading' ? 'animation: spin 1s linear infinite;' : ''\"\n            /\u003e\n            {{ toast.title }}\n          \u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e{{ toast.description }}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/svelte/toast'\n  import { X, LoaderIcon, CircleCheckIcon, CircleAlertIcon, InfoIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    overlap: true,\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  const uploadFile = () =\u003e {\n    return new Promise\u003cvoid\u003e((resolve, reject) =\u003e {\n      setTimeout(() =\u003e {\n        Math.random() \u003e 0.5 ? resolve() : reject(new Error('Upload failed'))\n      }, 2000)\n    })\n  }\n\n  const handleUpload = async () =\u003e {\n    toaster.promise(uploadFile, {\n      loading: {\n        title: 'Uploading file...',\n        description: 'Please wait while we process your file.',\n      },\n      success: {\n        title: 'Upload complete',\n        description: 'Your file has been uploaded successfully.',\n      },\n      error: {\n        title: 'Upload failed',\n        description: 'There was an error uploading your file. Please try again.',\n      },\n    })\n  }\n\n  const iconMap = {\n    loading: LoaderIcon,\n    success: CircleCheckIcon,\n    error: CircleAlertIcon,\n    info: InfoIcon,\n  }\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv\u003e\n  \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={handleUpload}\u003eUpload file\u003c/button\u003e\n\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cToaster {toaster}\u003e\n      {#snippet children(toast)}\n        {@const icon = toast().type ? iconMap[toast().type as keyof typeof iconMap] : InfoIcon}\n        \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e\n            \u003csvelte:component\n              this={icon}\n              class={styles.Indicator}\n              style={toast().type === 'loading' ? 'animation: spin 1s linear infinite;' : ''}\n            /\u003e\n            {toast().title}\n          \u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Update\n\nTo update a toast, use the `toast.update` method.\n\n**Example: update**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/react/toast'\nimport { useRef } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  overlap: true,\n  gap: 24,\n})\n\nexport const Update = () =\u003e {\n  const id = useRef\u003cstring\u003e(undefined)\n\n  const createToast = () =\u003e {\n    id.current = toaster.create({\n      title: 'Sending message...',\n      description: 'Please wait while we deliver your message.',\n      type: 'loading',\n    })\n  }\n\n  const updateToast = () =\u003e {\n    if (!id.current) {\n      return\n    }\n    toaster.update(id.current, {\n      title: 'Message sent',\n      description: 'Your message has been delivered successfully.',\n      type: 'success',\n    })\n  }\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"hstack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton type=\"button\" className={button.Root} onClick={createToast}\u003e\n        Send message\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cbutton type=\"button\" className={button.Root} onClick={updateToast}\u003e\n        Mark as sent\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root key={toast.id} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e{toast.title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e{toast.description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/solid/toast'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nexport const Update = () =\u003e {\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    overlap: true,\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  const [id, setId] = createSignal\u003cstring | undefined\u003e(undefined)\n\n  const createToast = () =\u003e {\n    const newId = toaster.create({\n      title: 'Uploading file...',\n      description: 'Please wait while your file is being uploaded.',\n      type: 'loading',\n    })\n    setId(newId)\n  }\n\n  const updateToast = () =\u003e {\n    const currentId = id()\n    if (!currentId) {\n      return\n    }\n    toaster.update(currentId, {\n      title: 'Upload complete',\n      description: 'Your file has been uploaded successfully.',\n      type: 'success',\n    })\n  }\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px' }}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onClick={createToast}\u003e\n          Start upload\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onClick={updateToast}\u003e\n          Complete upload\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/vue/toast'\nimport { X } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  overlap: true,\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nconst id = ref\u003cstring | undefined\u003e(undefined)\n\nconst createToast = () =\u003e {\n  id.value = toaster.create({\n    title: 'Uploading file...',\n    description: 'Please wait while your file is being uploaded.',\n    type: 'loading',\n  })\n}\n\nconst updateToast = () =\u003e {\n  if (!id.value) {\n    return\n  }\n  toaster.update(id.value, {\n    title: 'Upload complete',\n    description: 'Your file has been uploaded successfully.',\n    type: 'success',\n  })\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; gap: 8px\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton type=\"button\" :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"createToast\"\u003eStart upload\u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cbutton type=\"button\" :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"updateToast\"\u003eComplete upload\u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cToaster :toaster=\"toaster\" v-slot=\"toast\"\u003e\n        \u003cToast.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003e{{ toast.title }}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e{{ toast.description }}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/svelte/toast'\n  import { X } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    overlap: true,\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  let toastId: string | undefined = $state()\n\n  function createToast() {\n    toastId = toaster.create({\n      title: 'Uploading file...',\n      description: 'Please wait while your file is being uploaded.',\n      type: 'loading',\n    })\n  }\n\n  function updateToast() {\n    if (!toastId) {\n      return\n    }\n    toaster.update(toastId, {\n      title: 'Upload complete',\n      description: 'Your file has been uploaded successfully.',\n      type: 'success',\n    })\n  }\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv\u003e\n  \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; gap: 8px;\"\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={createToast}\u003eStart upload\u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={updateToast}\u003eComplete upload\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cToaster {toaster}\u003e\n      {#snippet children(toast)}\n        \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Action\n\nTo add an action to a toast, use the `toast.action` property.\n\n**Example: action**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/react/toast'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  gap: 24,\n})\n\nexport const Action = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        className={button.Root}\n        onClick={() =\u003e\n          toaster.create({\n            title: 'Event has been created',\n            description: 'We have sent you an email with the event details.',\n            type: 'info',\n            action: {\n              label: 'Undo',\n              onClick: () =\u003e {\n                console.log('Undo')\n              },\n            },\n          })\n        }\n      \u003e\n        Create event\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root key={toast.id} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e{toast.title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e{toast.description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              {toast.action \u0026\u0026 (\n                \u003cToast.ActionTrigger className={styles.ActionTrigger}\u003e{toast.action?.label}\u003c/Toast.ActionTrigger\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/solid/toast'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nexport const Action = () =\u003e {\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    overlap: true,\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        class={button.Root}\n        onClick={() =\u003e\n          toaster.create({\n            title: 'Invitation sent',\n            description: 'Your team invitation has been sent. Click undo to cancel.',\n            type: 'info',\n            action: {\n              label: 'Undo',\n              onClick: () =\u003e {\n                console.log('Undo clicked')\n              },\n            },\n          })\n        }\n      \u003e\n        Send invitation\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              {toast().action \u0026\u0026 (\n                \u003cToast.ActionTrigger class={styles.ActionTrigger}\u003e{toast().action?.label}\u003c/Toast.ActionTrigger\u003e\n              )}\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/vue/toast'\nimport { X } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  overlap: true,\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nconst addToast = () =\u003e {\n  toaster.create({\n    title: 'Invitation sent',\n    description: 'Your team invitation has been sent. Click undo to cancel.',\n    type: 'info',\n    action: {\n      label: 'Undo',\n      onClick: () =\u003e {\n        console.log('Undo clicked')\n      },\n    },\n  })\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"addToast\"\u003eSend invitation\u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cToaster :toaster=\"toaster\" v-slot=\"toast\"\u003e\n        \u003cToast.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003e{{ toast.title }}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e{{ toast.description }}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.ActionTrigger v-if=\"toast.action\" :class=\"styles.ActionTrigger\"\u003e\n            {{ toast.action?.label }}\n          \u003c/Toast.ActionTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/svelte/toast'\n  import { X } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    overlap: true,\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  function addToast() {\n    toaster.create({\n      title: 'Invitation sent',\n      description: 'Your team invitation has been sent. Click undo to cancel.',\n      type: 'info',\n      action: {\n        label: 'Undo',\n        onClick: () =\u003e {\n          console.log('Undo clicked')\n        },\n      },\n    })\n  }\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv\u003e\n  \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={addToast}\u003eSend invitation\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cToaster {toaster}\u003e\n      {#snippet children(toast)}\n        \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          {#if toast().action}\n            \u003cToast.ActionTrigger class={styles.ActionTrigger}\u003e{toast().action?.label}\u003c/Toast.ActionTrigger\u003e\n          {/if}\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Duration\n\nYou can control how long a toast stays visible by setting a custom `duration` in milliseconds, or use `Infinity` to keep\nit visible until manually dismissed.\n\n**Example: duration**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/react/toast'\nimport { XIcon, ClockIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  overlap: true,\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nconst durations = [\n  { label: '1s', value: 1000 },\n  { label: '3s', value: 3000 },\n  { label: '5s', value: 5000 },\n  { label: '∞', value: Infinity },\n]\n\nexport const Duration = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', flexWrap: 'wrap', gap: '8px' }}\u003e\n        {durations.map((duration) =\u003e (\n          \u003cbutton\n            key={duration.label}\n            type=\"button\"\n            className={button.Root}\n            onClick={() =\u003e\n              toaster.create({\n                title: 'Reminder set',\n                description: `This notification will ${\n                  duration.value === Infinity ? 'stay until dismissed' : `disappear in ${duration.label}`\n                }.`,\n                type: 'info',\n                duration: duration.value,\n              })\n            }\n          \u003e\n            {duration.label}\n          \u003c/button\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root key={toast.id} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e\n                \u003cClockIcon className={styles.Indicator} /\u003e\n                {toast.title}\n              \u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e{toast.description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/solid/toast'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst durations = [\n  { label: '1s', value: 1000 },\n  { label: '3s', value: 3000 },\n  { label: '5s', value: 5000 },\n  { label: '∞', value: Infinity },\n]\n\nexport const Duration = () =\u003e {\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    overlap: true,\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', 'flex-wrap': 'wrap', gap: '8px' }}\u003e\n        \u003cFor each={durations}\u003e\n          {(duration) =\u003e (\n            \u003cbutton\n              type=\"button\"\n              class={button.Root}\n              onClick={() =\u003e\n                toaster.create({\n                  title: `Duration: ${duration.label}`,\n                  description:\n                    duration.value === Infinity\n                      ? 'This toast will stay until you dismiss it.'\n                      : `This toast will automatically close in ${duration.label}.`,\n                  type: 'info',\n                  duration: duration.value,\n                })\n              }\n            \u003e\n              {duration.label}\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/For\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/vue/toast'\nimport { X } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  overlap: true,\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nconst durations = [\n  { label: '1s', value: 1000 },\n  { label: '3s', value: 3000 },\n  { label: '5s', value: 5000 },\n  { label: '∞', value: Infinity },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; flex-wrap: wrap; gap: 8px\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        v-for=\"duration in durations\"\n        :key=\"duration.label\"\n        type=\"button\"\n        :class=\"button.Root\"\n        @click=\"\n          toaster.create({\n            title: `Duration: ${duration.label}`,\n            description:\n              duration.value === Infinity\n                ? 'This toast will stay until you dismiss it.'\n                : `This toast will automatically close in ${duration.label}.`,\n            type: 'info',\n            duration: duration.value,\n          })\n        \"\n      \u003e\n        {{ duration.label }}\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cToaster :toaster=\"toaster\" v-slot=\"toast\"\u003e\n        \u003cToast.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003e{{ toast.title }}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e{{ toast.description }}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/svelte/toast'\n  import { X } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    overlap: true,\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  const durations = [\n    { label: '1s', value: 1000 },\n    { label: '3s', value: 3000 },\n    { label: '5s', value: 5000 },\n    { label: '∞', value: Infinity },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv\u003e\n  \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; flex-wrap: wrap; gap: 8px;\"\u003e\n    {#each durations as duration}\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        class={button.Root}\n        onclick={() =\u003e\n          toaster.create({\n            title: `Duration: ${duration.label}`,\n            description:\n              duration.value === Infinity\n                ? 'This toast will stay until you dismiss it.'\n                : `This toast will automatically close in ${duration.label}.`,\n            type: 'info',\n            duration: duration.value,\n          })}\n      \u003e\n        {duration.label}\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cToaster {toaster}\u003e\n      {#snippet children(toast)}\n        \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Max Visible\n\nSet the `max` prop on the `createToaster` function to define the maximum number of toasts that can be rendered at any\none time. Any extra toasts will be queued and rendered when a toast has been dismissed.\n\n**Example: max-toasts**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/react/toast'\nimport { XIcon, InfoIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  max: 3,\n  overlap: true,\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nexport const MaxToasts = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', flexWrap: 'wrap', gap: '8px' }}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          className={button.Root}\n          onClick={() =\u003e\n            toaster.create({\n              title: 'New notification',\n              description: 'You have a new message in your inbox.',\n              type: 'info',\n            })\n          }\n        \u003e\n          Add notification\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          className={button.Root}\n          onClick={() =\u003e {\n            const messages = [\n              'John liked your post',\n              'Sarah commented on your photo',\n              'New follower: @designpro',\n              'Your post was shared 10 times',\n              'Meeting reminder in 15 minutes',\n            ]\n            messages.forEach((msg) =\u003e {\n              toaster.create({\n                title: 'Notification',\n                description: msg,\n                type: 'info',\n              })\n            })\n          }}\n        \u003e\n          Add 5 notifications\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root key={toast.id} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cInfoIcon className={styles.Indicator} /\u003e\n              \u003cdiv style={{ flex: 1 }}\u003e\n                \u003cToast.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e{toast.title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n                \u003cToast.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e{toast.description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/solid/toast'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nexport const MaxToasts = () =\u003e {\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    max: 3,\n    overlap: true,\n    placement: 'bottom-end',\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', 'flex-wrap': 'wrap', gap: '8px' }}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          type=\"button\"\n          class={button.Root}\n          onClick={() =\u003e\n            toaster.create({\n              title: 'New notification',\n              description: 'Maximum of 3 toasts visible at once. Extra toasts are queued.',\n              type: 'info',\n            })\n          }\n        \u003e\n          Add toast\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n Sarah.' },\n              { title: 'File uploaded', description: 'Your document has been saved.' },\n              { title: 'Sync complete', description: 'All changes have been synced.' },\n              { title: 'New follower', description: 'John started following you.' },\n              { title: 'Task completed', description: 'Your export is ready for download.' },\n            ]\n            messages.forEach((msg) =\u003e {\n              toaster.create({\n                title: msg.title,\n                description: msg.description,\n                type: 'info',\n              })\n            })\n          }}\n        \u003e\n          Add 5 toasts\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/vue/toast'\nimport { X } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  max: 3,\n  overlap: true,\n  placement: 'bottom-end',\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nconst messages = [\n  { title: 'Message received', description: 'You have a new message from Sarah.' },\n  { title: 'File uploaded', description: 'Your document has been saved.' },\n  { title: 'Sync complete', description: 'All changes have been synced.' },\n  { title: 'New follower', description: 'John started following you.' },\n  { title: 'Task completed', description: 'Your export is ready for download.' },\n]\n\nconst addFiveToasts = () =\u003e {\n  messages.forEach((msg) =\u003e {\n    toaster.create({\n      title: msg.title,\n      description: msg.description,\n      type: 'info',\n    })\n  })\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; flex-wrap: wrap; gap: 8px\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        :class=\"button.Root\"\n        @click=\"\n          toaster.create({\n            title: 'New notification',\n            description: 'Maximum of 3 toasts visible at once. flex-wrap: wrap; gap: 8px;\"\u003e\n    \u003cbutton\n      type=\"button\"\n      class={button.Root}\n      onclick={() =\u003e\n        toaster.create({\n          title: 'New notification',\n          description: 'Maximum of 3 toasts visible at once. Extra toasts are queued.',\n          type: 'info',\n        })}\n    \u003e\n      Add toast\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cbutton\n      type=\"button\"\n      class={button.Root}\n      onclick={() =\u003e {\n        messages.forEach((msg) =\u003e {\n          toaster.create({\n            title: msg.title,\n            description: msg.description,\n            type: 'info',\n          })\n        })\n      }}\n    \u003e\n      Add 5 toasts\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cToaster {toaster}\u003e\n      {#snippet children(toast)}\n        \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Placement\n\nConfigure where toasts appear on the screen using the `placement` option in `createToaster`. Options include\n`top-start`, `top-end`, `bottom-start`, `bottom-end`, and more.\n\n**Example: placement**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/react/toast'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  placement: 'top-end',\n  overlap: true,\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nexport const Placement = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        className={button.Root}\n        onClick={() =\u003e\n          toaster.create({\n            title: 'Notification',\n            description: 'This toast appears at the top-right corner.',\n            type: 'info',\n          })\n        }\n      \u003e\n        Show toast (top-end)\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root key={toast.id} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e{toast.title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e{toast.description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/solid/toast'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nexport const Placement = () =\u003e {\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    placement: 'top-end',\n    overlap: true,\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        class={button.Root}\n        onClick={() =\u003e\n Show toast (top-end)\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cToaster toaster={toaster}\u003e\n          {(toast) =\u003e (\n            \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n              \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n              \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/vue/toast'\nimport { X } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\nconst toaster = createToaster({\n  placement: 'top-end',\n  overlap: true,\n  gap: 16,\n})\n\nconst addToast = () =\u003e {\n  toaster.create({\n    title: 'Notification',\n    description: 'This toast appears at the top-right corner.',\n    type: 'info',\n  })\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"addToast\"\u003eShow toast (top-end)\u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cToaster :toaster=\"toaster\" v-slot=\"toast\"\u003e\n        \u003cToast.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003e{{ toast.title }}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e{{ toast.description }}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Toast, Toaster, createToaster } from '@ark-ui/svelte/toast'\n  import { X } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/toast.module.css'\n\n  const toaster = createToaster({\n    placement: 'top-end',\n    overlap: true,\n    gap: 16,\n  })\n\n  function addToast() {\n    toaster.create({\n      title: 'Notification',\n      description: 'This toast appears at the top-right corner.',\n      type: 'info',\n    })\n  }\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv\u003e\n  \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={addToast}\u003eShow toast (top-end)\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cToaster {toaster}\u003e\n      {#snippet children(toast)}\n        \u003cToast.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e{toast().title}\u003c/Toast.Title\u003e\n          \u003cToast.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e{toast().description}\u003c/Toast.Description\u003e\n          \u003cToast.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cX /\u003e\n          \u003c/Toast.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Toast.Root\u003e\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Toaster\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n## Guides\n\n### Toast in Effects\n\nWhen creating a toast inside React effects (like `useEffect`, `useLayoutEffect`, or event handlers that trigger during\nrender), you may encounter a \"flushSync\" warning. To avoid this, wrap the toast call in `queueMicrotask`:\n\n```tsx\nimport { useEffect } from 'react'\n\nexport const EffectToast = () =\u003e {\n  useEffect(() =\u003e {\n    // ❌ This may cause flushSync warnings\n    // toaster.create({ title: 'Effect triggered!' })\n\n    // ✅ Wrap in queueMicrotask to avoid warnings\n    queueMicrotask(() =\u003e {\n      toaster.create({\n        title: 'Effect triggered!',\n        description: 'This toast was called safely from an effect',\n        type: 'success',\n      })\n    })\n  }, [])\n\n  return \u003cdiv\u003eComponent content\u003c/div\u003e\n}\n```\n\nThis ensures the toast creation is deferred until after the current execution context, preventing React's concurrent\nrendering warnings.\n\n### Styling\n\nThere's a minimal styling required for the toast to work correctly.\n\n#### Toast root\n\nThe toast root will be assigned these css properties at runtime:\n\n- `--x` - The x position\n- `--y` - The y position\n- `--scale` - The scale\n- `--z-index` - The z-index\n- `--height` - The height\n- `--opacity` - The opacity\n- `--gap` - The gap between toasts\n\n```css\n[data-scope='toast'][data-part='root'] {\n  translate: var(--x) var(--y);\n  scale: var(--scale);\n  z-index: var(--z-index);\n  height: var(--height);\n  opacity: var(--opacity);\n  will-change: translate, opacity, scale;\n  transition:\n    translate 400ms,\n    scale 400ms,\n    opacity 400ms,\n    height 400ms,\n    box-shadow 200ms;\n  transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.21, 1.02, 0.73, 1);\n\n  \u0026[data-state='closed'] {\n    transition:\n      translate 400ms,\n      scale 400ms,\n      opacity 200ms;\n    transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.06, 0.71, 0.55, 1);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Styling based on type\n\nYou can also style based on the `data-type` attribute.\n\n```css\n[data-scope='toast'][data-part='root'] {\n  \u0026[data-type='error'] {\n    background: red;\n    color: white;\n  }\n\n  \u0026[data-type='info'] {\n    background: blue;\n    color: white;\n  }\n\n  \u0026[data-type='warning'] {\n    background: orange;\n  }\n\n  \u0026[data-type='success'] {\n    background: green;\n    color: white;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Mobile considerations\n\nA very common use case is to adjust the toast width on mobile so it spans the full width of the screen.\n\n```css\n@media (max-width: 640px) {\n  [data-scope='toast'][data-part='group'] {\n    width: 100%;\n  }\n\n  [data-scope='toast'][data-part='root'] {\n    inset-inline: 0;\n    width: calc(100% - var(--gap) * 2);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Root Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | toast |\n| `[data-part]` | root |\n| `[data-state]` | \"open\" | \"closed\" |\n| `[data-type]` | The type of the item |\n| `[data-placement]` | The placement of the toast |\n| `[data-align]` |  |\n| `[data-side]` |  |\n| `[data-mounted]` | Present when mounted |\n| `[data-paused]` | Present when paused |\n| `[data-first]` |  |\n| `[data-sibling]` |  |\n| `[data-stack]` |  |\n| `[data-overlap]` | Present when overlapping |\n\n\n**ActionTrigger their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**CloseTrigger Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Description Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `duration` | `number` | No | The duration of the toast.\nBy default, it is determined by the type of the toast. |\n| `gap` | `number` | No | The gap between the toasts |\n| `hotkey` | `string[]` | No | The hotkey that will move focus to the toast group |\n| `max` | `number` | No | The maximum number of toasts. When the number of toasts exceeds this limit, the new toasts are queued. |\n| `offsets` | `string | Record\u003c'top' | 'bottom' | 'left' | 'right', string\u003e` | No | The offset from the safe environment edge of the viewport |\n| `overlap` | `boolean` | No | Whether to overlap the toasts |\n| `pauseOnPageIdle` | `boolean` | No | Whether to pause toast when the user leaves the browser tab |\n| `placement` | `Placement` | No | The placement of the toast |\n| `removeDelay` | `number` | No | The duration for the toast to kept alive before it is removed.\nUseful for exit transitions. |\n\n\n**Title Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Toaster Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `toaster` | `CreateToasterReturn` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `dir` | `'ltr' | 'rtl'` | No | The document's text/writing direction. |\n| `getRootNode` | `() =\u003e Node | ShadowRoot | Document` | No | A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments.
